***распространяться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распространяться.html>распространя́ться</a> (4983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распространять.html>распространя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasprostranjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распространяться.html>распространя́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasprostranjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распространиться.html>распространи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spread, to extend</li>
<li>to apply</li>
<li>to enlarge, to expatiate, to dilate</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распространять.html>распространя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasprostranjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распрощаться.html>распроща́ться</a> (10845)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощаться.html>проща́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proščátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распрощаться.html>распроща́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasproščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощаться.html>проща́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bid farewell, to say goodbye</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">распроститься</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rasprostitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ща́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:прощаться.html>проща́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>рас-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-прощ-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распря.html>ра́спря</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rásprja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распря.html>ра́спри</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распря.html>ра́спри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распря.html>ра́спрей</a></b>)

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прям</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ля́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***распускать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a> (11156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspuskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dismiss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собрание.html>собра́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspuskátʹ</b> sobránije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dismiss a meeting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to disband
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парламент.html>парла́мент</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspuskátʹ</b> parláment</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dissolve parliament</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspuskátʹ</b> komándu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pay off the crew</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каникулы.html>кани́кулы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspuskátʹ</b> na kaníkuly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dismiss for the holidays; break up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to loosen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspuskátʹ</b> pójas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to loosen the belt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to let out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знамя.html>знамёна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspuskátʹ</b> znamjóna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spread/unfurl the colours/banners</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspuskátʹ</b> vólosy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let one's hair down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвост</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:павлин.html>павли́не</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspuskátʹ</b> xvost (o pavlíne)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spread one's tail</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a> ню́ни</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">raspuskátʹ njúni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to snivel; slobber; whimper</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">raspuskátʹ rúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">let loose with one's fists; not to keep one's hands to oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">raspuskátʹ jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blab; blabber; not to watch one's tongue</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dissolve, to melt</li>
<li>to unknit</li>
<li>to untuck, to let out</li>
<li>to allow to get out of hand, to let get out of hand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сы́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>raspuskájet</b> svojevó sýna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is losing control of his son</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to set afloat, to spread
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слух.html>слух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspuskátʹ</b> slux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set a rumour afloat</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распускаться.html>распуска́ться</a> (18000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspuskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распускаться.html>распуска́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspuskátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распуститься.html>распусти́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(plants)</i> to open, to blossom out</li>
<li>to become loose, to unloosen, to slacken</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become undisciplined, to get out of hand</li>
<li>to dissolve, to melt</li>
<li><i>(woolen cloth)</i> to get/come unravelled</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspuskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пус<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:распуститься.html>распусти́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>рас-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-пуск-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***распустить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a> (6306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspustítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dismiss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собрание.html>собра́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspustítʹ</b> sobránije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dismiss a meeting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to disband
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парламент.html>парла́мент</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspustítʹ</b> parláment</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dissolve parliament</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspustítʹ</b> komándu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pay off the crew</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каникулы.html>кани́кулы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspustítʹ</b> na kaníkuly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dismiss for the holidays; break up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to loosen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspustítʹ</b> pójas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to loosen the belt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to let out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знамя.html>знамёна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspustítʹ</b> znamjóna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spread/unfurl the colours/banners</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspustítʹ</b> vólosy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let one's hair down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвост</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:павлин.html>павли́не</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspustítʹ</b> xvost (o pavlíne)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spread one's tail</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a> ню́ни</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">raspustítʹ njúni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to snivel; slobber; whimper</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">raspustítʹ rúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">let loose with one's fists; not to keep one's hands to oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">raspustítʹ jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blab; blabber; not to watch one's tongue</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dissolve, to melt</li>
<li>to unknit</li>
<li>to untuck, to let out</li>
<li>to allow to get out of hand, to let get out of hand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сы́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>raspustíl</b> svojevó sýna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has lost control of his son</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to set afloat, to spread
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слух.html>слух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspustítʹ</b> slux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set a rumour afloat</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сти́ть</b>

Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:распускать.html>распуска́ть</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распуститься.html>распусти́ться</a> (12524)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распуститься.html>распусти́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspustítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распускаться.html>распуска́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(plants)</i> to open, to blossom out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:березка.html>берёзка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:распуститься.html>распусти́лась</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">berjózka ješčó ne <b>raspustílasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the birch tree has not come out [broken into leaf] yet; the birch is not yet in leaf</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become loose, to unloosen, to slacken</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become undisciplined, to get out of hand</li>
<li>to dissolve, to melt</li>
<li><i>(woolen cloth)</i> to get/come unravelled</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распутица.html>распу́тица</a> (26210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">putʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распутица.html>распу́тица</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspútica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распутица.html>распу́тицы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распутица.html>распу́тицы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распутица.html>распу́тиц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>season of impassable roads</li>
<li>impassable roads, flooded roads</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распутье.html>распу́тье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspútʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распутье.html>распу́тья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распутье.html>распу́тья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распутье.html>распу́тий</a></b>)

***распухнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распухнуть.html>распу́хнуть</a> (9640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пухнуть.html>пу́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">púxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распухнуть.html>распу́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspúxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пухнуть.html>пу́хнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распухать.html>распуха́ть</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распустить.html>распу́щенный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspúščennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распущенность.html>распу́щенность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspúščennostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распущенность.html>распу́щенности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распущенность.html>распу́щенности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распущенность.html>распу́щенностей</a></b>)
